CQDemand: changes in customer purchasing behaviour, volumes, pricing power, discounting, delayed purchasing, routes to market? B

- DC bandwidth demand grew +330% (2020-24) with hyperscaler capex acceleration confirming the structural shift [J]

- Hyperscaler 2025 capex plans: Meta $60bn+, Google $50bn+, Microsoft $80bn+ [I]

- HTRO Q4 DC organic growth +62% confirms demand pull is live [A]

- AI/ML inference workloads adding a second leg of structural demand [A]
CQCompetition: changes in industry structure, competitive intensity, new entrants, market share dynamics, barriers to entry/exit, competitor financial health? C

- Cable/connectivity industry consolidating with HTRO holding stable mid-market position [J]

- Prysmian dominant at top end (EUR 16bn rev); HTRO niche operator at SEK 7.5bn [I]

- Chinese competitive entrants in FS pricing aggressive but contained to commodity segments [A]
CQDisruption: technology disruption, innovative new entrants, substitute offerings, disintermediation? C

- DC technology stable; FS substitution by 5G/satellite a real but slow threat over 5+ years [J]

- Optical fibre still dominant for hyperscaler interconnect; no near-term substitute [I]

- FS broadband substitution risk concentrated in marginal markets [A]
CQPolitical/regulatory: actual or plausible political and regulatory influence across geographies and sector? B

- EU Gigabit Infrastructure Act (force May 2024) provides structural FS demand floor [J]

- German broadband EUR 38bn vs EUR 12bn prior commitment [I]

- EU Digital Decade target: 100% Gigabit coverage by 2030 [I]
CQSupply side: changes in supplier economics, relationships, concentration, risks, financial health? C

- Supplier base stable: copper/optical fibre commodities sourced through long-term contracts [J]

- No single-source supplier concentration risk identified [I]

- Input cost volatility manageable within 200-300bp gross margin band [A]
CQRevenue/demand cycle: cyclicality, predictability, stage of cycle, end-market data beyond company commentary? C

- FS in early upcycle; DC structurally non-cyclical (AI capex secular), HE niche stable [J]

- FS organic -1% FY25 reading like trough; EU subsidy disbursement supports recovery [A]

- DC bandwidth demand growth secular, not cyclical (AI/ML training + inference) [A]
CQMacroeconomic: broad macro forces on revenue growth and margins over L18M and N3Y? C

- ECB rate-cutting cycle tailwind for leverage cost (1.9x); EUR/SEK volatility minor [J]

- Interest rate cycle elevated through 2025 weighed on financing costs [I]

- Forward EUR/SEK assumed ~stable; no large translation hit modelled [A]

CQLeadership: changes in CEO, CFO, IR, board, 2nd-level management, culture, employee turnover? B

- CEO Fröberg (Mar 2025): external hire from McKinsey, Ahlsell, Ansell signals strategy reset [J]

- Deputy CEO Åberg provides continuity; reduces key-man risk through transition [I]

- CFO Pernilla Linden continuing; segment EBITA disclosure from Q1 2025 is governance signal [I]
CQStrategy/structure: changes in corporate strategy, strategic priorities, financial goals, org structure, core/non-core perimeter, M&A posture, partnerships/JVs, activism? C

- Three-pronged: PIP (SEK 110m/yr benefit) + M&A velocity (JOWO Q2 2026) + DC scaling [J]

- PIP: SEK 230m one-off cost, SEK 110m/yr recurring benefit; in execution Q3 2025+ [A]

- 20+ acquisitions 2020-24 still need integration discipline; first real test [A]
CQPriorities/ambition: changes in ambition intensity, values, standards, productivity, behaviours: CEO verbal commentary tone and energy? B

- Mgmt 2028 targets are ambitious: SEK 11bn rev / 12% EBITA margin (vs FY25 9.4%) [J]

- New CEO commentary tone: operationally focused, segment-by-segment [I]

- Corporate change is real but <18M old; needs 2 quarters of margin proof [A]
CQFinancial profile: changes in growth rates, margins, leverage, cash conversion, FCF, shareholder returns, investment intensity (opex/capex/intangibles), benchmarked vs competitors? C

- Margin trajectory: gross 42.2% (2023) to 38.5% (2025); recovery requires DC mix accretion [J]

- DC EBITA 15.3% vs group 9.4% Q4 2025: every 5pp mix shift adds 50bp at group [A]

- Capex intensity low (2-3% of sales), preserving FCF for dividends + bolt-on M&A [A]
CQTrack record of delivery: guidance vs actuals vs sell-side over L3Y: financial, strategic, operational delivery, internal vs external cause delineation? C

- Mixed: strong DC build from zero to SEK 1.4bn but FS margin compression weighs [J]

- FS margin collapsed 2024; clear external cause (Chinese pricing) but operator response slow [A]

- DC growth track record is the case-defining proof point: 39% Q3 then 62% Q4 organic [A]

CQ(Well-invested base?)? C

CQPast/present fundamental delivery congruency with thesis? C

- Good: historical narrative (acquisition to margin to diversification) extends naturally to current thesis [J]

CQLarge CfC/mispricing? C

- Moderate: CfC cleared substantially (CEO + PIP); residual mispricing 30-50% remains [J]

- Current EV/EBITDA 4.3x vs Prysmian 8-10x; ~50% discount excessive for 62% DC growth [A]

- Fair discount given execution risk + leverage = 20-30%; implies 30-50% upside re-rating [A]
CQLow trading multiple? B

- Yes: 4.3x EV/EBITDA / 1.0x EV/Sales / 1.4x P/B all below historical and peer averages [J]

- Peers: Prysmian 8-10x EV/EBITDA, Corning 12-14x [I]

- Discount magnitude excessive for company with 62% DC organic + structural tailwind [A]
